table: wordsearch

drop table if exists wordsearch;

create table wordsearch (
    word VARCHAR(5) not null,
    char1 VARCHAR(1) not null,
    char2 VARCHAR(1) not null,
    char3 varchar(1) not null,
    char4 varchar(1) not null,
    char5 varchar(1) not null,
    common varchar(1) not null
);

	-- id INT NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
    word VARCHAR(5) not null,
    char1 VARCHAR(1) not null,
    char2 VARCHAR(1) not null,
    char3 varchar(1) not null,
    char4 varchar(1) not null,
    char5 varchar(1) not null,
    common varchar(1) not null
    -- primary key (id)
);
